country_event = { # Strike
	id = ukrpol.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.6" }
	title = ukrpol.6.t
	desc = ukrpol.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_strike

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_path
			}
		}
		UKR_decrease_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_minor_concessions
			days = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			UKR_increase_king_strength = yes
			UKR_increase_workers_opinion_king = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_increase_workers_opinion_hetman = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
		}
		227 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.07
		UKR_decrease_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_general_strike
			days = 14
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			clear_variable = UKR_workers_alignment
			UKR_increase_king_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_king = yes
			UKR_increase_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			clear_variable = UKR_workers_alignment
			UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
			UKR_increase_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.6.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
		}
		227 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 1
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1
			}
		}
		UKR_increase_direktoria = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_general_strike_big
			days = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_king_path }
			clear_variable = UKR_workers_alignment
			UKR_decrease_king_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_king = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_king = yes
		}
		else = {
			clear_variable = UKR_workers_alignment
			UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
			UKR_decrease_Protofis_opinion_hetman = yes
		}
	}
}

			set_nationality = ROOT

		}

			clr_country_flag = UPR_melnyk_on_our_side
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = -0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = 0.03
			}

				event_target:UKR_Mykola_Stsiborskyi = {
					promote_leader = yes

					set_unit_leader_flag = UVO_Galicia_leader
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = leftist_uvo_becomes_dominant_galicia
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mykola Stsiborskyi"
				desc = "POLITICS_MYKOLA_STSIBORSKYI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Mykola_Stsiborskyi.png"

				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
		}
		else = {

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.38" }
	title = ukrpol.38.t
	desc = ukrpol.38.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_dyrektoria_arrives

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.38.a
		set_global_flag = UPR_dyrektoria_joined_peacefully
		clr_country_flag = UKR_dyrektoria_uprising_active
		remove_ideas = UKR_political_instability
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
				UPR = { become_exiled_in = { target = WSU legitimacy = 0.35 } }
			}
			UPR = {
				event_target:UPR_Joint_Command = { retire = yes }
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = UKR
				}
			}
			WSU = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = UKR_uvo_officer
					}
					set_nationality = UKR
				}
			}
			clear_variable = UKR_Direktoriia_Strength
			clear_global_event_target = UKR_dyrektoria_headquarters
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}		
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.38.b
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}	
}
country_event = { # hidden event for ai UPR
	id = ukrpol.10000
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.40" }
	title = ukrpol.40.t
	desc = ukrpol.40.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		GAL = { 
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.39
				days = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { country_exists = CRM } }
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.54
				days = 20
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = UKR_dnieper_explosion }
			UPR = {
				AUS = {
					country_event = {
						id = ukrpol.41
						days = 7
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = UKR_hetmanate_is_over }
			UPR = {
				GER = {
					country_event = {
						id = ukrpol.52
						days = 7
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ukrpol.58
			days = 5
		}
	}	
}

		effect_tooltip = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_trait = UKR_uga_officer }
				set_nationality = FROM
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_trait = UKR_uga_officer }
				set_nationality = XXA
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrpol.40
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}	
}

country_event = { # Crimea
	id = ukrpol.54
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.54" }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CRM = { 
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes 
				add_ideas = CRM_crimean_tatar_rule
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CRM_Amet_Ozenbashly_hog_sli
					CRM_Asan_Sabri_Ayvazov_for_sli
					CRM_Usein_Abdurefi_Bodaninskiy_eco_sli
					CRM_Seitcelli_Usein_Hattat_sec_sli
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal
				}
				set_temp_variable = { soccon_pop = ROOT.party_popularity@social_conservative }
				multiply_temp_variable = { soccon_pop = 100 }
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					popularity = soccon_pop
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0
				}
				unlock_national_focus = CRM_Crimean_Regional_Government
				unlock_national_focus = CRM_Secure_The_Perekop_Isthmus
				unlock_national_focus = CRM_Appeal_To_German_Mediation
				unlock_national_focus = CRM_Independence
				unlock_national_focus = CRM_Push_Towards_Federation
			}
		}
	}
	title = ukrpol.54.t
	desc = ukrpol.54.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.54.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_crimea_will_revolt
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 137
					state = 1220
					state = 1221
				}
			}
			set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			hidden_effect = { add_core_of = CRM }
			force_enable_resistance = {
				occupied = CRM
				occupier = 202.owner
			}
			start_resistance = yes
			set_resistance = 20
		}
	}

country_event = { # Regency Council
	id = ukrpol.121
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.121" }
	title = ukrpol.121.t
	desc = ukrpol.121.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.121.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_regency_leo_stefan > UKR_regency_danilo }
					check_variable = { UKR_regency_leo_stefan > UKR_regency_pavlo }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_regency_pavlo > UKR_regency_danilo }
					check_variable = { UKR_regency_pavlo > UKR_regency_leo_stefan }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_will_become_hetmanate }
				}
			}
		}
		UKR_create_leo_stefan = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_will_become_hetmanate }
			set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_hetmanate
			add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
			hidden_effect = {
				get_current_government_type = yes
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = market_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
			hidden_effect = {
				get_current_government_type = yes
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = market_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_king_title
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = UKR_regency_council
		set_country_flag = UKR_regency_council_over
		country_event = {
			id = ukrpol.122
			days = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.121.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_regency_pavlo > UKR_regency_danilo }
			check_variable = { UKR_regency_pavlo > UKR_regency_leo_stefan }
			has_country_flag = UKR_will_become_hetmanate
		}
		add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
		set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_hetmanate
		set_country_leader_portrait = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			portrait = GFX_Portrait_UKR_Pavlo_Skoropadskyi_Hetman
		}
		set_country_leader_description = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			desc = POLITICS_PAVLO_SKOROPADSKYI_DESC
		}
		clr_country_flag = UKR_regency_council
		set_country_flag = UKR_regency_council_over
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.121.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_regency_danilo > UKR_regency_pavlo }
			check_variable = { UKR_regency_danilo > UKR_regency_leo_stefan }
		}
		UKR_create_danylo = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_will_become_hetmanate }

			add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
			hidden_effect = {
				get_current_government_type = yes
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = market_liberal }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				set_politics = { ruling_party = social_conservative }
				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title

				add_country_leader_trait = UKR_hetman_title
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
			}
		}
		else = {

country_event = { # Czernin Agreements
	id = ukrpol.164
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrpol.164" }
	title = ukrpol.164.t
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.164.d.faction
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_AUS_alliance }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrpol.164.d.buffer
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_AUS_buffer }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrpol.164.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_AUS_alliance }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 91
					state = 89
					state = 80
					state = 1140
					state = 1127
					state = 1126
					state = 713
				}
				is_owned_and_controlled_by_AUS_or_subject = yes
			}
			UKR = { 
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_claim = PREV
				hidden_effect = { remove_state_claim = 713 }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = AUS
					modifier = KR_returned_land
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			add_to_faction = UKR
		}
		else = {
			create_faction = dniep_danubian_alliance
			add_to_faction = UKR
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = POL
					tag = GAL
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = AUS
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = UKR
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = UKR_AUS_alliance
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrpol.164.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_AUS_buffer }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 91
					state = 89
					state = 80
					state = 1140
					state = 1127
					state = 1126
				}
				is_owned_and_controlled_by_AUS_or_subject = yes
			}
			WSU = { 
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
				WSU_create_buffer_zone = yes
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				state = 713 
				is_owned_and_controlled_by_AUS_or_subject = yes
			}
			BUK = {
				transfer_state = 713
				add_state_core = 713
				get_current_government_type = yes
			}
			AUS = {
				puppet = BUK
			}
			BUK = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
		}
		AUS = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = UKR
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = WSU
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = WSU
				relation = guarantee
				active = yes
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = WSU
				relation = military_access
				active = yes
			}
		}
		UKR = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = WSU
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = WSU
				relation = guarantee
				active = yes
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = WSU
				relation = military_access
				active = yes
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {

				OR = {

			}

				id = ukrsun.13
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.67 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ukrsoc.67.t
	desc = ukrsoc.67.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_for_sender = no

	major = yes
	show_major = {
		has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote }}
			wants_world_news = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#that's a damn shame
		name = ukrsoc.67.a
	}
}

country_event = { # Kyiv Conference
	id = ukrsoc.69
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.69" }
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.69.t.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.69.t.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.69.d.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.69.d.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.69.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = 25
		set_global_flag = KCN_economic_yes
		KCN_add_to_kcn_economic = yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote }
			}
			country_event = ukrsoc.71
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
					OR = {
						GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
						is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = THIS }
						is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 2 }
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.KCN_voters
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.70 days = KCN_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
							is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = THIS }
							is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 2 }
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.KCN_voters
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.71 days = KCN_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
			}
		}			
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.69.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
	}	
}
country_event = { # Kyiv Conference
	id = ukrsoc.70
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.70" }
	title = ukrsoc.70.t
	desc = ukrsoc.70.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.70.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
					is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = THIS }
					is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
				}
			}
		}			
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_1
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_2
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_3
			}
		}
		GER_leave_mitteleuropa = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research }
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = ROOT } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_withdraws_from_sphere
			hidden_effect = { country_event = japfor.404 }
			JAP = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_outraged }
				country_event = japfor.409
			}
			remove_ideas = JAP_nav_tra_idea
		}
		KCN_add_to_kcn_economic = yes
	}	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.70.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
					is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = THIS }
					is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
				}
			}
		}		
	}		
}

			base = 50

				factor = 0
				has_socialist_government = no
				has_left_democratic_government = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				has_government = totalist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				has_democratic_socialist_government = yes
			}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_1
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_2
				has_idea = JAP_member_integration_3
			}

			limit = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research }
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
		}

			limit = { is_in_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = ROOT } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_withdraws_from_sphere
			hidden_effect = { country_event = japfor.404 }
			JAP = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = KR_outraged }
				country_event = japfor.409
			}
			remove_ideas = JAP_nav_tra_idea

		KCN_add_to_kcn_economic = yes

		name = ukrsoc.71.b

				factor = 15
				has_socialist_government = no
				has_left_democratic_government = no
			}

				factor = 15

					OR = {
						GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes

	}

country_event = { # Kyiv Conference
	id = ukrsoc.72
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.72" }
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.72.t.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.72.t.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.72.d.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.72.d.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.72.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = 25
		set_global_flag = KCN_research_yes			
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = kyiv_conf_research
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote }
			}
			country_event = ukrsoc.73
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
					is_in_tech_research_group = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 2 }
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.KCN_voters
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.73 days = KCN_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
					is_in_tech_research_group = no
				}
				set_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 2 }
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.KCN_voters
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.74 days = KCN_vote_delay }
					add_to_temp_variable = { KCN_vote_delay = 1 }
				}
			}
		}			
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.72.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
	}	
}

			base = 70
			modifier = {

			}
		}

			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = russian_research
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = german_research
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = phalanstere_research
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = entente_research
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = us_research
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = japan_research
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = austrian_research

			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = belgian_research
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = argentina_research
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = balkan_research

			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = CHI_KR_research_tech_group
			remove_from_tech_sharing_group = cubcos_research

		}
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = kyiv_conf_research

			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				is_in_tech_research_group = yes
			}
		}		
	}

country_event = { #KCN offers us an alliance
	id = ukrsoc.75
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.75" }
	title = ukrsoc.75.t
	desc = ukrsoc.75.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.75.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				has_socialist_government = no
				has_left_democratic_government = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = hosts_kyiv_conference
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = KCN_allied_@ROOT
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.76
				days = 3
				random = 72
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.75.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = KCN_allied_@FROM }
		}
		set_country_flag = KCN_alliance_refused_@FROM
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_socialist_government = no
				has_left_democratic_government = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KCN_refused_kcn_participation
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.76
				days = 3
				random = 72
			}
		}
	}	
}

country_event = { #Country responds
	id = ukrsoc.76
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.76" }

	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.76.t.accept
		trigger = { has_country_flag = KCN_allied_@FROM }
	}
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.76.t.refuse
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = KCN_allied_@FROM } }
	}

	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.76.d.accept
		trigger = { has_country_flag = KCN_allied_@FROM }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.76.d.refuse
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = KCN_allied_@FROM } }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.76.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = KCN_allied_@FROM
		}
		clr_country_flag = KCN_allied_@FROM
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = KCN_initialize_country_accept }
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.76.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = KCN_allied_@FROM }
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Membership - voting
	id = ukrsoc.77
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.77 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ukrsoc.77.t
	desc = ukrsoc.77.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = KCN_vote_yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#No
		name = KCN_vote_no
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_no_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		name = KCN_vote_abstain
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_abstain_votes = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Kyiv Conference
	id = ukrsoc.79
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.79" }
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.79.t.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	title = {
		text = ukrsoc.79.t.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.79.d.yes
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukrsoc.79.d.no
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.79.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes } }
		event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = {
			KCN_add_to_kcn_council = yes
			country_event = ukrsoc.80
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				country_event = ukrsoc.56
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = KCN_candidate_membership
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.79.b
		trigger = { check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes < global.kcn_no_votes } }
		add_political_power = -25
		event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = {
			country_event = ukrsoc.81
		}
		clear_global_event_target = KCN_candidate_membership
	}	
}

country_event = { #Membership - voting
	id = ukrsoc.85
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.85 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ukrsoc.85.t
	desc = ukrsoc.85.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yes
		name = KCN_vote_yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#No
		name = KCN_vote_no
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { any_owned_state = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				any_owned_state = { 
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
						is_core_of = event_target:KCN_candidate_membership
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_government_type_as_ROOT_authoritarian = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_no_votes = 1 }
	}

	option = {	#Abstain
		name = KCN_vote_abstain
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:KCN_candidate_membership = { same_continent_as_ROOT = no }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { global.kcn_abstain_votes = 1 }
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.113" }
	title = ukrsoc.113.t
	desc = ukrsoc.113.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.113.a
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_in_faction_with = INT }
			}
			INT = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		}
		else = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			give_guarantee = FROM
			FROM = { give_guarantee = ROOT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { has_government = totalist }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				name = UKR_radical_socialist_party3
				long_name = UKR_radical_socialist_party3_long
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mykola Skrypnyk"
				desc = "POLITICS_MYKOLA_SKRYPNYK_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Mykola_Skrypnyk.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = national_communism_subtype
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.117
				days = 180
				random_days = 300
			}
		}
	}		
}

country_event = { # USDRP
	id = ukrsoc.152
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrsoc.152" }
	title = ukrsoc.152.t
	desc = ukrsoc.152.d
		
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_no_more_loans }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget > 0 }
				check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget < 11 }
			}
			check_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget < 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.152.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_pop_change = -10 }
		UKR_increase_red_kyiv_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate
				days = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Navodnytskyi_Mist }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Navodnytskyi_Mist
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Renovate_Velykyi_Mykola }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Renovate_Velykyi_Mykola
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Karl_Marx_Monument }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Karl_Marx_Monument
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Metro_Construction }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Metro_Construction
				days = 150
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Open_Shevchenko_State_Art_School }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Open_Shevchenko_State_Art_School
				days = 15
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line
				days = 30
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrsoc.152
				days = 90
				random_days = 220
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_Borrow_money_tt
		add_to_variable = { var = UKR_kyiv_budget_debt value = 40 }
		multiply_variable = { UKR_kyiv_budget_debt = 1.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Repay_money }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = UKR_Repay_money
				days = 180
			}
		}
		else = { activate_mission = UKR_Repay_money }
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrsoc.152.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}		
		set_country_flag = UKR_no_more_loans
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 25
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_pop_change = 5 }
		UKR_increase_red_kyiv_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_budget_monthly_change = -5 }
		UKR_increase_kyiv_budget_monthly_by_sum = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full }
			remove_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_full
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate }
			remove_mission = UKR_Great_Constructions_moderate
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Metro_Construction }
			add_days_remove = {
				decision = UKR_Metro_Construction
				days = 150
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line }
			remove_decision = UKR_Launch_The_First_Trolleybus_Line
		}		
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_red_kyiv_budget_change = 40 }
		UKR_increase_kyiv_budget_by_sum = yes
	}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukreco.14" }
	title = ukreco.14.t
	desc = ukreco.14.d

		UKR = { has_country_flag = UKR_famine }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukreco.14.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_decrease_risk_of_famine
		add_to_variable = { UKR_risk_of_famine_var = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { UKR_famine_monthly_population = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { UKR_famine_stability_factor = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { UKR_famine_war_support_factor = 0.08 }
		add_to_variable = { UKR_famine_consumer_goods_factor = -0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { UKR_famine_industrial_capacity_factory = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { UKR_famine_conscription_factor = 0.06 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_risk_of_famine_var < 1 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = ukreco.19
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { UKR_debt_burden = 1 }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = UKR_pay_off_debt }
	}		
}

		}

			factor = 80

				days = 4

}

		remove_state_core = 791
		remove_state_core = 78
		remove_state_core = 1222
		UKR = {
			transfer_state = 78
			transfer_state = 1222
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 192
			}

				transfer_state = 192
			}
		}
		if = {

				owns_state = 791
			}

			}

country_event = { # Ukraine into the world
	id = ukraine.81
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukraine.81" }
	title = ukraine.81.t
	desc = ukraine.81.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_UKR_kulaks_angry
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ukraine.81.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 66
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_faction_leader = no
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = UKR_foreign_policy
								option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_NEUTRALITY
							}
						}
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_foreign_policy
						option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_FACTION_LEADER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = UKR_Splendid_Isolation
			add_idea = UKR_Splendid_Isolation_2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				GER = {
					country_event = {
						days = 4
						id = ukraine.74
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = POL
					POL = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				}
				POL = { country_event = poland.234 }
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ukraine.81.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_foreign_policy
						option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_NEUTRALITY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_foreign_policy
						option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_FACTION_LEADER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			is_faction_leader = no
			is_in_faction = yes
		}
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ukraine.81.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_government = national_populist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_foreign_policy
						option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_NEUTRALITY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = UKR_foreign_policy
						option = UKR_FOREIGN_POLICY_FACTION
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
				GER = {
					country_event = {
						days = 4
						id = ukraine.74
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = no
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = no }

		}

				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat

					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes

country_event = { #PS - Czechoslovakia Result
	id = ukrfor.27
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.27" }
	title = ukrfor.27.t
	desc = ukrfor.27.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = ukrfor.27.a
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
			set_country_flag = czechoslovakia_independent_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
			set_country_flag = czechoslovakia_separate_approved
		}
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = ukrfor.27.b
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
		clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
		set_country_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_denied
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #PS - Galicia Result
	id = ukrfor.31
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.31" }
	title = ukrfor.31.t
	desc = ukrfor.31.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = ukrfor.27.a
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
			set_country_flag = galicia_split_ukraine_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
			set_country_flag = galicia_split_russia_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
			set_country_flag = galicia_annex_russia_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
			set_country_flag = eastgalicia_split_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
			set_country_flag = eastgalicia_ukraine_approved
		}
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = ukrfor.27.b
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
		clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Free Czechoslovakia
	id = ukrfor.1305
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.1305" }
	title = ukrfor.1305.t
	desc = ukrfor.1305.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1305.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = czechoslovakia_independent_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZE
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Johann II zu Schwarzenberg"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						has_country_flag = CZE_SVK_was_puppeted
						}
					}
					effect_tooltip = { kill_country_leader = yes }
				}
			set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_czechoslavakia
			
			leave_faction = yes
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = czechoslovakia_separate_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZE
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CZE
				}
					CZE = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Johann II zu Schwarzenberg"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							has_country_flag = CZE_SVK_was_puppeted
							}
						}
						effect_tooltip = { kill_country_leader = yes }
					}
				
				leave_faction = yes
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SVK = { is_subject_of = AUS }
				}
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = SVK
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
				SVK = { 
					leave_faction = yes
					separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SVK = { NOT = { owns_state = 664 } }
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = 664
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				AUS = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = SVK
						}
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = SVK
						}
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = zakarpatie_cze_approved }
			}
			CZE = {
				transfer_state = 73
				transfer_state = 1119
				add_state_core = 73
				add_state_core = 1119
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = zakarpatie_slo_approved }
			}
			SVK = {
				transfer_state = 73
				transfer_state = 1119
				add_state_core = 73
				add_state_core = 1119
			}
		}
	}
}	
country_event = { #Austria tries to release our territory
	id = ukrfor.1306
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.1306" }
	title = ukrfor.1306.t
	desc = ukrfor.1306.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1306.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1306.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { owns_state = 73 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { owns_state = 70 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { owns_state = 875 }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		AUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.1307
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Hungary outraged
	id = ukrfor.1307
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.1307" }
	title = ukrfor.1307.t
	desc = ukrfor.1307.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1307.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		HUN = { add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = KR_disapproves_of_govt
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = ukrfor.1305
					days = 1
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				country_event = {
					id = ukrfor.1308
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	} 
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1307.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukrfor.1312
				days = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = austria_refuse_to_release_czechs
		}
	}
}

	desc = ukrfor.1308.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1308.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { owns_state = 73 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { owns_state = 70 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { owns_state = 875 }
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			AUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = HUN
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			leave_faction = yes
			load_oob = HUN_AUS_Civil_war
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = "Ten new militia divisions will be formed"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = AUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		country_event = kr.hungary.2
	}
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1308.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Russia agrees
	id = ukrfor.1326
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ukrfor.1326" }
	title = ukrfor.1310.t
	desc = ukrfor.1326.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ukrfor.1326.a
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CRO }
			SER = { 
				annex_country = {
					target = CRO
					transfer_troops = yes
				} 
			}
		}
		else = {
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = CRO
						}
					}
					SER = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						state = 102
					}
					SER = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = AUS
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
